This test verifies that the exception is NOT caught (the bug)\n        with pytest.raises(adblock.DeserializationError):\n            ad_blocker.read_cache()\n\n        # If the exception was properly handled, message.error would be called\n        # But since the exception is unhandled, this assertion will fail\n        # when the bug is fixed\n        mock_error.assert_not_called()\n\n\ndef test_corrupted_cache_should_be_handled_gracefully(\n    temp_data_dir,\n    corrupted_cache_file,\n    monkeypatch,\n):\n    \"\"\"Test that corrupted cache is properly handled (expected behavior after fix).\n\n    This test documents what SHOULD happen: the application should gracefully\n    handle corrupted cache files by logging an error and continuing.\n\n    Currently this test is expected to fail because the bug prevents proper\n    error handling.\n    \"\"\"\n    ad_blocker = braveadblock.BraveAdBlocker(data_dir=temp_data_dir)\n\n    # Mock message.error to verify error is shown\n    with mock.patch.object(qute_message, 'error') as mock_error:\n        # After the fix, this should NOT raise an exception\n        # Instead, it should call message.error with an appropriate message\n        try:\n            ad_blocker.read_cache()\n            # If we reach here, the fix is in place\n            mock_error.assert_called_once()\n            call_args = mock_error.call_args[0][0]\n            assert \"Reading adblock filter data failed\" in call_args\n        except adblock.DeserializationError:\n            # This is the current (buggy) behavior\n            pytest.fail(\n                \"DeserializationError was not caught. \"\n                \"The read_cache() method should handle corrupted cache files gracefully.\"\n            )\n\n\ndef test_various_corrupted_cache_formats(temp_data_dir):\n    \"\"\"Test that various types of corrupted cache cause the same unhandled exception.\"\"\"\n    corrupted_data_samples = [\n        b\"\",  # Empty file\n        b\"\\x00\" * 100,  # All null bytes\n        b\"random garbage data\",  # Random text\n        b\"\\xff\\xfe\\xfd\\xfc\",  # Binary garbage\n        b\"{\"+'valid json but not cache data'\"}\",  # Instead, the exception propagates unhandled.\n    \"\"\"\n    from qutebrowser.components import braveadblock\n    from qutebrowser.api import config, message\n\n    # Create a BraveAdBlocker instance pointing to our temp directory\n    # The read_cache() method should handle the corrupted cache gracefully\n        # by catching the DeserializationError and showing an error message.\n        # However, due to the bug, it will raise an unhandled DeserializationError.\n\n        # This test verifies that the exception is NOT caught (demonstrates the bug)\n        with pytest.raises(adblock.DeserializationError):\n            ad_blocker.read_cache()\n\n        # If the exception was properly handled, message.error would be called\n        # But since the exception is unhandled, this assertion passes\n        # when the bug exists (exception is not caught)\n        mock_error.assert_not_called()\n\n\ndef test_corrupted_cache_should_be_handled_gracefully(\n    temp_data_dir,\n    corrupted_cache_file,\n):\n    \"\"\"Test that corrupted cache is properly handled (expected behavior after fix).\n\n    This test documents what SHOULD happen: the application should gracefully\n    handle corrupted cache files by logging an error and continuing.\n\n    Currently this test demonstrates that the bug exists - the exception\n    is not caught and propagates unhandled.\n    \"\"\"\n    from qutebrowser.components import braveadblock\n    from qutebrowser.api import config, message\n\n    with mock.patch.object(config, 'val') as mock_config_val:\n        mock_config_val.content.blocking.method = 'adblock'\n        mock_config_val.content.blocking.enabled = True\n        mock_config_val.content.blocking.adblock.lists = []\n\n        ad_blocker = braveadblock.BraveAdBlocker(data_dir=temp_data_dir)\n\n    #
